2026-07-08 01:54:56  ASSISTANT:        Selection reporting verified exactly: text, `inMainPanel`, and source
                                       lines 20–20, alongside top/bottom visible lines. The feature is
                                       complete and working end to end. Here's the shape of it:

                                       **The `state` tool** (`mcp__ui__state`, allowed alongside `ui`): as
                                       you said, it's just a tool that awaits a response over the websocket
                                       — it opens a short-lived connection to the back end, sends
                                       `state:request`, and the back end forwards it to browser clients; the
                                       first `state:response` is routed back (10s server timeout, 15s tool
                                       timeout so it can never hang). The reply becomes JSON text content,
                                       plus an MCP **image block** when `screenshot: true` (reusing the same
                                       `captureMainView` the camera button uses, so annotations are
                                       included).

                                       **What the snapshot contains**
                                       - **Open file**: mode (viewing/authoring), URL, filename, file type —
                                       or in authoring mode, the current merged OUI program (capped at 8k
                                       chars).
                                       - **Scroll with line numbers**: pixels, percent, and
                                       `topSourceLine`/`bottomSourceLine`. This came from a new rehype
                                       plugin (`rehypeSourceLines`) that stamps every rendered markdown
                                       element with `data-source-line` from remark's position info (sanitize
                                       schema updated to let the attribute through) — so the DOM is
                                       addressable by source line.
                                       - **Selection**: text (capped 4k), whether it's inside the main
                                       panel, and its **start/end source lines**.
                                       - **Pointer**: position, how stale it is, and the element under it
                                       (tag, source line, text preview).
                                       - Extras I added that you didn't list: **chat panel open/busy**,
                                       **drawing mode + stroke count**, **viewport size**, and a timestamp.
                                       The system prompt tells Claude to call it before answering questions
                                       about "this/here/what's on screen."

                                       **Things I noticed, for your list**
                                       - **Multiple tabs race**: with two browsers connected (yours + my
                                       automation tab), first response wins — one of my probes was actually
                                       answered by *your* window. Fine for now; a "most recently active
                                       client" preference would fix it.
                                       - **OUI documents have no line numbers** — stamps are markdown-only.
                                       The natural OUI equivalent is which `statementId`s are visible /
                                       which tab is active in a rendered `Tabs`; the parser retains
                                       statementIds, so that's feasible follow-up.
                                       - Other candidates worth adding later: the **document's raw text**
                                       around the selection (context window), **active OUI tab labels**,
                                       chat scroll position, and the doc's load error state.
                                       - A UX note from testing: real mouse selections survive focus moving
                                       to the chat input (the "selection cleared" scares in my testing were
                                       an automation artifact — verified selections persist 6+ seconds
                                       in-page).

                                       Uncommitted for now — it's interleaved with your other worker's
                                       in-flight App/toolbar changes again, so tell me when and how you want
                                       it sliced.

                                       S = os.environ['S']
                                       def rd(n): return open(f'{S}/{n}').read()
                                       def wr(n, s): open(f'{S}/{n}', 'w').write(s)
                                       def sub1(s, old, new):
                                           assert s.count(old) == 1, f'not unique or missing: {old[:60]!r}'
                                           return s.replace(old, new)

                                       LogCommand;',
                                       '''export type ClientMessage =
                                         | ChatCommand
                                         | LogCommand
                                         | StateRequestCommand
                                         | StateResponseCommand;

                                       /**
                                        * Front-end state inspection. The LLM's `state` MCP tool connects to
                                       the
                                        * websocket and sends state:request; the back end forwards it to
                                       browser
                                        * clients, and the first state:response with a matching id is routed
                                       back
                                        * to the requester.
                                        */
                                       export interface StateRequestCommand {
                                         type: "state:request";
                                         id: string;
                                         /** Also capture a screenshot of the main window (PNG data URL). */
                                         screenshot?: boolean;
                                       }

                                       export interface StateResponseCommand {
                                         type: "state:response";
                                         id: string;
                                         /** Structured snapshot of what the user is looking at. */
                                         state?: unknown;
                                         /** PNG data URL of the main window, when requested. */
                                         screenshot?: string;
                                         error?: string;
                                       }''')
                                       pr = sub1(pr, '''  | UiStartEvent
                                         | UiDeltaEvent
                                         | UiSpecEvent;''',
                                       '''  | UiStartEvent
                                         | UiDeltaEvent
                                         | UiSpecEvent
                                         | StateRequestEvent
                                         | StateResponseEvent;

                                       /** state:request forwarded to browser clients (shape mirrors the
                                       command). */
                                       export interface StateRequestEvent {
                                         type: "state:request";
                                         id: string;
                                         screenshot?: boolean;
                                       }

                                       /** state:response routed back to the requesting client. */
                                       export interface StateResponseEvent {
                                         type: "state:response";
                                         id: string;
                                         state?: unknown;
                                         screenshot?: string;
                                         error?: string;
                                       }''')
                                       wr('protocol.c2.ts', pr)

                                       ch = sub1(ch, '  private readonly uiBlocks = new Map<number, { raw:
                                       string; sent: number }>();',
                                       '''  private readonly uiBlocks = new Map<number, { raw: string; sent:
                                       number }>();
                                         /** In-flight state:request ids → the client awaiting the response.
                                       */
                                         private readonly pendingState = new Map<
                                           string,
                                           { requester: WebSocket; timer: NodeJS.Timeout }
                                         >();''')
                                       ch = sub1(ch, '''    this.logger.log("client", message as unknown as
                                       Record<string, unknown>);

                                           switch (message.type) {''',
                                       '''    // Screenshot data URLs are large; log their size, not their
                                       content.
                                           const loggable =
                                             message.type === "state:response" && message.screenshot
                                               ? { ...message, screenshot: `<data url,
                                       ${message.screenshot.length} chars>` }
                                               : message;
                                           this.logger.log("client", loggable as unknown as Record<string,
                                       unknown>);

                                           switch (message.type) {
                                             case "state:request": {
                                               this.onStateRequest(ws, message.id, message.screenshot ===
                                       true);
                                               return;
                                             }
                                             case "state:response": {
                                               const pending = this.pendingState.get(message.id);
                                               if (!pending) return; // late or duplicate answer
                                               clearTimeout(pending.timer);
                                               this.pendingState.delete(message.id);
                                               this.sendTo(pending.requester, {
                                                 type: "state:response",
                                                 id: message.id,
                                                 state: message.state,
                                                 screenshot: message.screenshot,
                                                 error: message.error,
                                               });
                                               return;
                                             }''')
                                       ch = sub1(ch, '  /** Translate one raw Claude CLI stream event into
                                       chat:* events. */',
                                       '''  /**
                                          * Forward a state request to browser clients (everyone but the
                                       requester);
                                          * the first matching state:response wins. Times out after 10s so
                                       the MCP
                                          * tool never hangs.
                                          */
                                         private onStateRequest(
                                           requester: WebSocket,
                                           id: string,
                                           screenshot: boolean
                                         ): void {
                                           const browsers = [...this.clients].filter(
                                             (c) => c !== requester && c.readyState === c.OPEN
                                           );
                                           if (browsers.length === 0) {
                                             this.sendTo(requester, {
                                               type: "state:response",
                                               id,
                                               error: "no front-end client is connected",
                                             });
                                             return;
                                           }
                                           const timer = setTimeout(() => {
                                             this.pendingState.delete(id);
                                             this.sendTo(requester, {
                                               type: "state:response",
                                               id,
                                               error: "front end did not respond within 10s",
                                             });
                                           }, 10_000);
                                           this.pendingState.set(id, { requester, timer });
                                           const payload = JSON.stringify({ type: "state:request", id,
                                       screenshot });
                                           for (const browser of browsers) browser.send(payload);
                                         }

                                         /** Translate one raw Claude CLI stream event into chat:* events.
                                       */''')
                                       wr('chat.c2.ts', ch)
